  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer5179990926876042372"><b>Deep in the heart of Texas, Morganville is a small college town full of laid-back students and eccentric townies, not to mention the sort of creatures you wouldn't want to run into after dark. Despite their obvious differences, the human and vampire residents of Morganville have learned to coexist, but that doesn't stop genius student Claire Danvers from keeping up her gua</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5179990926876042372" style="display:none"><b>Deep in the heart of Texas, Morganville is a small college town full of laid-back students and eccentric townies, not to mention the sort of creatures you wouldn't want to run into after dark. Despite their obvious differences, the human and vampire residents of Morganville have learned to coexist, but that doesn't stop genius student Claire Danvers from keeping up her guard. Because in Morganville, nothing is as it seems...</b><br /><br />While developing a new system to maintain the town's defenses, Claire discovers a way to use the vampires' powers to help keep outsiders from spreading news of Morganville's "unique" situation once they've crossed the city limits.<br /><br />But the new system has an unexpected and possibly deadly consequence: People inside the town start forgetting who and what they are - even the vampires. And when Claire's boyfriend, Shane, and her best friend, Eve, start treating her like a perfect stranger, Claire realizes she has to figure out a way to pull the plug on her experiment - before she forgets how to save herself... and Morganville.</span>

    <a title="Jessica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3283298-jessica"><img alt="Jessica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572125481p2/3283298.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/117049905?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica" href="/user/show/3283298-jessica">Jessica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3283298-jessica?shelf=0-faves">0-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3283298-jessica?shelf=15-vampires">15-vampires</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer117049905" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3914629144289340661">Alright, let's see if I can come up with a spoiler-free review.<br/><br/>The Morganville Vampires series is one of those which I've put off reading for quite a while. Somehow I just expected myself not to like it. I had "Glass Houses" sitting on my shelf for months before I finally picked it up but as it turned out, I fell in love immediately. And who would have thought, 9 books later I am <i>still</i> loving it. I guess what makes this series one of my favorites are the characters and their close friendship. I </span>
  <span id="freeText3914629144289340661" style="display:none">Alright, let's see if I can come up with a spoiler-free review.<br /><br />The Morganville Vampires series is one of those which I've put off reading for quite a while. Somehow I just expected myself not to like it. I had "Glass Houses" sitting on my shelf for months before I finally picked it up but as it turned out, I fell in love immediately. And who would have thought, 9 books later I am <i>still</i> loving it. I guess what makes this series one of my favorites are the characters and their close friendship. I just love the entire gang, how they always stick together and how they make up their own little family. I love their house, how it seems to have a mind of its own and how it's comforting and protecting its residents. And then there's Myrnin of course. Crazy Myrnin, who always makes me laugh. These books are just full of interesting and loveable characters!<br /><br />Ok, enough of the general rambling. What to say about this 9th installment without giving anything away? Just like all the other books in this series this was a nice and quick read, with some good laughs and a healthy dose of drool-worthy Shane moments. The story itself was gripping and kept me turning pages quickly. There were some small things that bugged me (plotwise) but when it comes to the Morganville Vampires I somehow seem to be able to overlook the occasional flaw.<br />All in all, I enjoyed Ghost town immensely even though it made me cry and ends on a sad note, which I’m not very fond of. <br />I know I've wreaked some havoc with my comments (sorry Nic and Tina) but I really can't say anything else about this book before you guys haven't read it, too. But don't worry too much, I'm sure you're going to love it :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3914629144289340661" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14908877705550439229">yay! more of myrnin!!!<br/>what can I say.. i like the guy<br/><br/><i>Kissa's Review</i><br/><br/>ah Myrnin... you insane twisted vampire, you have really screwed up this time...<br/><br/>Okay, i don't want to give any spoilers out, so i'll keep it as informationally non-informational as possible.. if that makes sense<br/><br/>So, basically, Morganville is still it's weird, scary, vampire-fied town, but this book in the series really gets into some scary stuff... i'm talking brain in a jar freaky... i mean really?! but that's why i love the plac</span>
  <span id="freeText14908877705550439229" style="display:none">yay! more of myrnin!!!<br />what can I say.. i like the guy<br /><br /><i>Kissa's Review</i><br /><br />ah Myrnin... you insane twisted vampire, you have really screwed up this time...<br /><br />Okay, i don't want to give any spoilers out, so i'll keep it as informationally non-informational as possible.. if that makes sense<br /><br />So, basically, Morganville is still it's weird, scary, vampire-fied town, but this book in the series really gets into some scary stuff... i'm talking brain in a jar freaky... i mean really?! but that's why i love the place: its insane vampires.<br /><br />Book 9 of the Morganville Vampire series really starts going when Claire gets into some trouble (of course). She's got to get punished, which i find completely unjustified by the way, but Amelie has got to "do what's best for Morganville." Hence comes the 'working with her half-crazy vampire boss' part. This is all pretty early on, it's the basis of the rest of the plot, so pay attention to it... at which point Claire sleeps in Myrnin's bed... *wolf whistle* <br /><br />And then we move on from there and the real complication begins, and Claire finds herself alone and feels like she's not really apart of Morganville at all... confusing, i know, but i promised <i>no spoilers!</i><br /><br />Oh God, the madness in that place never ends... i'd really rather not spill any more details, cos i wouldn't want to give out any spoilers, but that place is so crazy, and <i>now</i> Claire has to fix something that's messing with memories <i>in the wrong way</i>.. which is just plain terrifying.. <br /><br />Characters: Amelie is still mysterious, Oliver is still the sarcastic (for me: loveable) jerk he's always been, Myrnin is still the good 'ol most insane guy on the block (and we love him for it). Same story for everyone else, not much has changed with the characters, except we sort of catch a tiny, miniscule, punicated glipse of Oliver at a vulnerable moment, and even a bit of past information about Myrnin is revealed.... but i aint tellin you any o that! read it!<br /><br />Overall: <b>Ghost Town</b> i'm thinking, is one of my favourites in the series... it has heaps of Myrnin in it and his fluffy bunny fang slippers, and the plot doesn't crawl at a snail's pace (thank god!)... it's another typical Morganville adventure that proves that Caine still has some good ideas in that head of hers, and that Claire and the gang just can<i>not</i> catch a break, with a whole lotta action, a few make-out sessions (ooo), and some humour in between, plus <i>of course</i> scenes with Myrnin... sum it all up = Ghost Town</span>
  <a data-text-id="14908877705550439229" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_93715351" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/93715351" />
    <a title="Literary Ames {Against GR Censorship}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2109885-literary-ames-against-gr-censorship"><img alt="Literary Ames {Against GR Censorship}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1297107033p2/2109885.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/93715351?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Literary Ames {Against GR Censorship}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Literary Ames {Against GR Censorship}" href="/user/show/2109885-literary-ames-against-gr-censorship">Literary Ames {Against GR Censorship}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780749008048" href="/book/show/7913590-ghost-town">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2109885-literary-ames-against-gr-censorship?shelf=dtb">dtb</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2109885-literary-ames-against-gr-censorship?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2109885-literary-ames-against-gr-censorship?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2109885-literary-ames-against-gr-censorship?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2109885-literary-ames-against-gr-censorship?shelf=read-in-2010">read-in-2010</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer93715351" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13395516327236339141">Oh, Myrnin. Myrnin, Myrnin, Myrnin. Excuse my language but you fucked up, dude. I worried for your sanity and for your life. There were times when I loved you and when I hated you. You've caused so much trouble, so much pain and suffering and yet I still care about you. Even on that last page when my jaw dropped after my little fit of worry over what you may have done to yourself.<br/><br/><i>Ghost Town</i> really begins when Claire stakes and kills a vamp whilst trying to rescue Eve and is sentenced to no sleep</span>
  <span id="freeText13395516327236339141" style="display:none">Oh, Myrnin. Myrnin, Myrnin, Myrnin. Excuse my language but you fucked up, dude. I worried for your sanity and for your life. There were times when I loved you and when I hated you. You've caused so much trouble, so much pain and suffering and yet I still care about you. Even on that last page when my jaw dropped after my little fit of worry over what you may have done to yourself.<br /><br /><i>Ghost Town</i> really begins when Claire stakes and kills a vamp whilst trying to rescue Eve and is sentenced to no sleep or rest of any kind until she's fixed the machine that runs Morganville, previously run by Ada. And while she manages it by the skin of her teeth, Myrnin tweaks it for his own purposes which causes both humans and vampires, one by one, to lose their memories of the last 3 years. <br /><br />As a result, all hell breaks loose with the hero in the end being someone you wouldn't expect but it was a redeeming act. Only the last page twists things to the point where I'm not sure whether Myrnin's actions were good (as it may provide much needed closure and no one was killed) or just plain bad but I worry about the effect it will have on a couple of the characters.<br /><br />I know this took me a few days to finish but this is no reflection of the book itself but rather a severe lack of free time. I enjoyed it more than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7248501.Kiss_of_Death__Morganville_Vampires___8_" title="Kiss of Death (Morganville Vampires, #8) by Rachel Caine" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Death</a> partly because there was less cringe-worthy kissy-wissy lovey-doveyness between Shane and Claire, instead these kinds of moments were made to be sweet and endearing. In fact, a couple of my favourites are when Shane starts falling for Claire again when he can't remember any of their previous time together and when Claire does the same. <br /><br />I want to quickly comment on the Myrnin-Claire possibility which I've previously noted in earlier reviews. This possibility is noted by several characters in this book plus Myrnin is unusually kind and caring towards Claire and makes comparisons between her and Ada who he admits was his lover. Also, Claire sleeps in his bed! Not that I want this to happen, I love Shane but I just think he might make a move on her at some point in the future.<br /><br />Another thing I loved about this book was the politics, specifically the relationship between Amelie and Oliver and the town. It's complicated but one of the lessons I've learned is never be complacent when you're in a position of power, it leads to humiliating circumstances. And, um, never fall in love with your rival?<br /><br />Also included in my UK edition was a short story called <b>
  <i>'Worth Living For'</i>
</b> from Shane's perspective set between <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6670348.Fade_Out__The_Morganville_Vampires___7_" title="Fade Out (The Morganville Vampires, #7) by Rachel Caine" rel="nofollow noopener">Fade Out</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7248501.Kiss_of_Death__Morganville_Vampires___8_" title="Kiss of Death (Morganville Vampires, #8) by Rachel Caine" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of Death</a> involving Michael and Bishop. The story sees Shane approached and asked to secretly follow Michael when it looks like he may be helping Bishop who has escaped and on the run. It's not a great story and isn't important to the overall story in the main books. And if you were wondering, the title <i>'Worth Living For'</i> refers to Claire, of course. ;)</span>
  <a data-text-id="13395516327236339141" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2487371050" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2487371050" />
    <a title="Helen Power" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5877123-helen-power"><img alt="Helen Power" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1549247071p2/5877123.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2487371050?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Helen Power" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Helen Power" href="/user/show/5877123-helen-power">Helen Power</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5877123-helen-power?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5877123-helen-power?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2487371050" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6424730200752842515">We’re back to Morganville for the ninth instalment of the Morganville Vampires book series!<br/><br/>Vampires and humans coexist (somewhat) peacefully in the sleepy town of Morganville, Texas.  During the day, Claire Danvers attends the local university, but at night she works for the mad, genius vampire Myrnin in his lab, where he mixes alchemy with science.  In this installment of the series, Claire and Myrnin "fix" the town’s security system, which insures that anyone who leaves Morganville immediately</span>
  <span id="freeText6424730200752842515" style="display:none">We’re back to Morganville for the ninth instalment of the Morganville Vampires book series!<br><br>Vampires and humans coexist (somewhat) peacefully in the sleepy town of Morganville, Texas.  During the day, Claire Danvers attends the local university, but at night she works for the mad, genius vampire Myrnin in his lab, where he mixes alchemy with science.  In this installment of the series, Claire and Myrnin "fix" the town’s security system, which insures that anyone who leaves Morganville immediately forgets about its <i>
  uniqueness
</i>--namely, the fact that vampires roam the streets at night.  But something goes terribly wrong, and everyone starts to forget who they are. The fact that Claire’s boyfriend doesn’t recognize her is bad enough, but when vampires forget what they are and start to lose their inhibitions? Not yet plagued by memory loss, Claire must seek unlikely assistance in saving Morganville from itself.<br><br>I enjoyed this installment in the series, but I realized that I’m really starting to dislike the vampires, and it’s making me dislike Claire for wanting to protect them.  Early in the book, Claire kills a vampire <i>
  in self defence
</i>, yet she is severely punished for it, because vampire lives are worth more than human lives in this twisted, messed-up reality.  I wouldn’t mind this fact <i>
  at all
</i> if the vampires weren’t so whiny about it.  They’re very much “we’re the victims, despite the fact that we kill you all the time and don’t respect human lives at all”.  And it’s not in a psychopathic, only my feelings matter sort of way. It’s in a whiny, toddler-mentality sort of way. It’s very frustrating. In other books, like the Sookie Stackhouse series, at least the vampires are extremely narcissistic, egotistical, badass, and evil. Somehow what Caine is trying to do, making the vampires vulnerable, makes them seem spineless and, quite frankly, annoying. This has resulted in me strongly disliking all the  vampires, with the obvious exception of Myrnin, because he’s fabulous and wonderful and beautifully insane, which makes up for the boring monotony of Amelie and Oliver. I wouldn’t mind if Amelie and Oliver were to leave the entire series and we focused on Myrnin and his delightful weirdness for a book or two.<br><br>That said, this book featured some interesting character development for Amelie and Oliver. <strong>It shows that even vampires can learn life lessons.  </strong>They’re revealed as being capable of change, despite not having aged for hundreds of years.<br><br>The Morganville vampire series is still <strong>a young adult romance at heart</strong>, and it features some adorable scenes between Claire and her boyfriend, Shane. It’s heartbreaking when he forgets who she is, but this makes it even more satisfying when he trusts her and protects her while she tries to save the town.  At points it was a little <i>
  too 
</i>cheesy, particularly when Eve and Michael (Claire's roommates) who are in love but don’t remember it, profess their crushes to each other. In the middle of a life-or-death situation.  I think it was meant to be cute, but it was really quite ridiculous.  But, to be honest, it was kind of accurate. Gotta love teenage hormones.<br><br>Another thing I love about this book series is the recaps at the beginning. Since the books jump into things without much preamble, it makes it easier for those who haven’t read the series in a while, or those who haven’t read the previous books, to understand what’s happening. There’s nothing worse than getting halfway through a book which you haven’t read the previous installment in years, and suddenly having a critical piece of information revealed to you--something that would have changed the way you interpreted the entire first half of the book. The book's forward provides everything you need to know about the town, its idiosyncrasies, without too many major spoilers for what happened in the previous books. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1538944185i/26414642.jpg" alt="Ghost Town Book review" width="300" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>I recommend this book to those who want to read about vampires, but not about romance with vampires.</strong> Claire falls in love with a human boy, but she's still navigating a dangerous world filled with blood-sucking monsters. She's also a relatable main character in the sense that she's very human, very vulnerable, and a bit of a nerd.  Although, sometimes I think she's <em>too </em>good, and I would like to see her go on a vampire killing spree. I guess I'll just have to rewatch <em>Buffy the Vampire Slayer </em>if I want to see that.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1536888492i/26298996.png" alt="star" width="35" height="36" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1536888492i/26298996.png" alt="star" width="35" height="36" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1536888492i/26298996.png" alt="star" width="35" height="36" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><em> This review appeared first on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://powerlibrarian.wordpress.com/">https://powerlibrarian.wordpress.com/</a> </em></span>
  <a data-text-id="6424730200752842515" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

      <span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_review_2487371050'><a id="like_count_review_2487371050" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/2487371050?resource_type=Review"><span class="likesCount">14 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it gr-button gr-button--small" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F7600922-ghost-town">Like</a></span>

<div id="review_100693076" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/100693076" />
    <a title="Arlene" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene"><img alt="Arlene" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347048609p2/1746727.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/100693076?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arlene" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arlene" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene">Arlene</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=read-2010">read-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=ya-paranormal">ya-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer100693076" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17887859566142082812">Rachel Caine has once again delivered a wild adventure in Morganville filled with crazy twists, snark-worthy dialog and a perfect set of characters that kept me glued to every page. I loved <b>Ghost Town</b> and after waiting six long months for this book and devouring it in a few short hours, I’m back to anticipating the release of the next installment. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8799269.Bite_Club__The_Morganville_Vampires__10_' title='Bite Club (The Morganville Vampires,#10) by Rachel Caine' rel='nofollow noopener'>Bite Club</a> can’t get here fast enough!!<br/><br/>There was plenty of action in this book and squee-worthy Claire and Shane moments that had me re-reading paragra</span>
  <span id="freeText17887859566142082812" style="display:none">Rachel Caine has once again delivered a wild adventure in Morganville filled with crazy twists, snark-worthy dialog and a perfect set of characters that kept me glued to every page. I loved <b>Ghost Town</b> and after waiting six long months for this book and devouring it in a few short hours, I’m back to anticipating the release of the next installment. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8799269.Bite_Club__The_Morganville_Vampires__10_" title="Bite Club (The Morganville Vampires,#10) by Rachel Caine" rel="nofollow noopener">Bite Club</a> can’t get here fast enough!!<br /><br />There was plenty of action in this book and squee-worthy Claire and Shane moments that had me re-reading paragraphs at a time. Myrnin made me laugh, kept me on edge and broke my heart all in a matter of a few hundred pages. As always, I never know what to expect from him besides a shoe collection that has me searching the internet for his style of <a href="http://www.bunnyslippers.com/bunny-slippers/killer-rabbit-slippers.php" rel="nofollow noopener">slippers</a>. Shane was perfect as always in this book. I love his relationship with Claire and his friendship with Eve and Michael. Michael, oh Michael, there never seems to be enough of him in any of the books. What a great set of characters that blend and contrast in all the right ways. <br /><br />Ghost Town doesn’t waste any time taking off with a heavy dose of insane and wild. Claire Danvers is developing a new system to maintain Morganville’s defenses, but the result has unexpected consequences. As soon as the system is activated humans and vampires in the town of Morganville suffer from memory lapse, which creates a full on epidemic of hysteria. While the town is turned upside down, the power shift between Amelie and Oliver causes additional chaos where Claire, Shane, Michael and Eve must work together to bring order back to their town all the while trying to cope with their own memory loss.<br /><br />Reading these books puts me in a setting that feels familiar and full of crazy, which feels about right… every single time. There’s no denying… I’m addicted and I want more. If you’re a fan of vampire lore and love your stories filled with wild adventure, this series is a MUST and Ghost Town does not disappoint!<br /><br /><b>Favorite Quotes</b> Mostly Shane quotes BTW. :)<br />"I’m not dropping my pants,” Shane said. “I just thought I’d say that up front.”<br /><br /><br />'What’s snogging?” Shane asked. “Ridiculous displays of inappropriate affection in front of me. Roughly translated. And what are you doing here?” Myrnin was genuinely offended, Claire realized. Not good.<br /><br />"You are not a ninja, Shane." Claire said. "I watched all the movies. I just haven't gotten the certificate from the correspondence course yet." <br /><br /><br />Eve looked at Claire. "Really? Is he running for Worst Boyfriend Ever?" "In the subcategory of Completely Awesome," Shane said, and stole some of her fries.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17887859566142082812" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1045628002" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1045628002" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<span id="freeTextContainer15482482692889275389"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>This man wearing clothes from the OMG No store.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Ha. Myrnin had a pimp hat. Just when I didn't think he could surpass the vampire bunny slippers. I heart me some Myrnin. <br/><br/><b>3.5 stars</b>. If I hadn't been so bored with the first half of <i>Ghost Town</i>, this surely would have been a 4 star read for me because the last half had me glued to the virtual pages. So much awesome was crammed into those final chapters. I think the slow start/hectic finish might be a Morganville series thing because I've n</span>
  <span id="freeText15482482692889275389" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>This man wearing clothes from the OMG No store.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Ha. Myrnin had a pimp hat. Just when I didn't think he could surpass the vampire bunny slippers. I heart me some Myrnin. <br /><br /><b>3.5 stars</b>. If I hadn't been so bored with the first half of <i>Ghost Town</i>, this surely would have been a 4 star read for me because the last half had me glued to the virtual pages. So much awesome was crammed into those final chapters. I think the slow start/hectic finish might be a Morganville series thing because I've noticed that most of what I find entertaining about these books often tends to happen in the second half. It's entirely possible that there might be some pacing issues at work here. <br /><br />Oh well though. I was so surprised, impressed, and repelled by the solution to the "memory loss" issue that I'm excited to tear into book 10 to see how one certain person is going to handle THAT fallout. This is a good thing, especially considering how long it took for me to read book 9 after finishing book 8 (it was awhile). <br /><br />Yay for finally trying to finish this series after all of this time, haha. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15482482692889275389" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1459333580" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1459333580" />
    <a title="Carrie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36817401-carrie"><img alt="Carrie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415677371p2/36817401.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1459333580?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carrie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carrie" href="/user/show/36817401-carrie">Carrie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1459333580" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9931279517122043432">Ghost Town is the ninth book in the Morganville Vampire series by Rachel Caine. Picking up right after the last book, Claire and her friends need to save the town yet again after a fix for the computer system running Morganville doesn't go as planned and begins causing the residents to lose their memories. <br/><br/>A part of me enjoys this series then a part tends to think it's getting a bit repetitive at this point. Ghost Town was one of the better books of the series as some have seemed to drag quite a</span>
  <span id="freeText9931279517122043432" style="display:none">Ghost Town is the ninth book in the Morganville Vampire series by Rachel Caine. Picking up right after the last book, Claire and her friends need to save the town yet again after a fix for the computer system running Morganville doesn't go as planned and begins causing the residents to lose their memories. <br /><br />A part of me enjoys this series then a part tends to think it's getting a bit repetitive at this point. Ghost Town was one of the better books of the series as some have seemed to drag quite a bit but this one wasn't too bad in that regard. However, I do think it gets a bit silly by now that everyone seems to keep rushing off into danger and some of the action seems to be getting repeated over and over. <br /><br />In the end, decided on 3.5 stars for this installment. Still kind of funny and entertaining but I wonder how there's actually any new ideas to keep reading with so many books to go. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9931279517122043432" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_93772496" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/93772496" />
    <a title="~Tina~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2594672-tina"><img alt="~Tina~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411474324p2/2594672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/93772496?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Tina~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Tina~" href="/user/show/2594672-tina">~Tina~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=bite-me">bite-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=own-copy">own-copy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer93772496" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7852734729009215924"><b>SPOILER ALERT</b><br/><br/>I swear, Love, will never be a strong enough word to convey my feelings for this series. It's always a blast reading a Morganville book and I always miss them when there gone.<br/><br/>So, what's up this time in Morganville? Why, memory lost of course...;)<br/><br/>While Myrnin and Claire tweaked the machine to get the boundaries back up and running, I think either Claire's sleep deprived-ness or Myrnin's...well <i>Myrnin</i> might have missed a step.<br/>Bringing the town of Morganville back three years before an</span>
  <span id="freeText7852734729009215924" style="display:none"><b>SPOILER ALERT</b><br /><br />I swear, Love, will never be a strong enough word to convey my feelings for this series. It's always a blast reading a Morganville book and I always miss them when there gone.<br /><br />So, what's up this time in Morganville? Why, memory lost of course...;)<br /><br />While Myrnin and Claire tweaked the machine to get the boundaries back up and running, I think either Claire's sleep deprived-ness or Myrnin's...well <i>Myrnin</i> might have missed a step.<br />Bringing the town of Morganville back three years before and driving them down a notch to crazier, it's up to Claire to set things right before her memories goes poof like the rest of them.<br /><br /><b>Ghost Town</b> is another awesome addition to the world of crazy plots and insane characters. I had a lot of fun with this since it was interesting to see how things would pan out with the foursome and see how they'd interact with each other now. Some of it was very sad and I really felt bad for Shane and what he had to relive. Same goes for Myrnin he broke my heart with some of the touching things he did. <i>"I'll be your hands"</i>. He may have mucked things up pretty good in this one, but I absolutely love that whack-o!!<br />Lots of Shane-Swoon worthy moments here, even while his memory was affected he's still...<i>Shane</i> and I simply adore <s>all his nakedness</s> him to bits.<br /><br />While these books are very much <i>out there</i> it truly doesn't matter to me in the least. They are entertaining, fun and quirky as hell. I love that there is always something up in Morganville, but by the time the book is done, it's solved (more or less). I get my dose of crazy without having to pull my hair out with the cliffies. It's just one of the best things about this series, besides, it's freaken addicting!<br />I'll never get tired of there wit and banter that Caine flawlessly delivers in ever book she pens.<br />But that ending? Oh.Crap. I so don't wanna know how that black-hole of a secret is gonna effect my favorite couple. I'm nervous just thinking about it.<br /><br />As always, this was another fantastic and amazing installment that I can't ever seem to get enough of. Thank God we only have to wait six more months to get <i>Bite Club</i> in our greedy little hands.<br /><br />Forever love it! Need more!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7852734729009215924" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Kim" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1594906-kim"><img alt="Kim" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1252264728p2/1594906.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<span id="freeTextContainer5632280454849290601">I'll keep it short and <i>very</i> spoilery.<br/><br/>Myrnin and Claire managed to fix the machine to replace Ada. This version doesn't include someone's brain in a jar, of course. One <i>small</i> detail: It's flawed and instead of wiping people's memories after leaving Morganville, it just erases (almost) everybody's memories from the past 3 years.<br/><br/>Result: Myrnin is back to being a cruel lunatic and won't let anybody near his machine (he still thinks it's Ada in there), Amelie and Oliver don't get along, Michael refus</span>
  <span id="freeText5632280454849290601" style="display:none">I'll keep it short and <i>very</i> spoilery.<br /><br />Myrnin and Claire managed to fix the machine to replace Ada. This version doesn't include someone's brain in a jar, of course. One <i>small</i> detail: It's flawed and instead of wiping people's memories after leaving Morganville, it just erases (almost) everybody's memories from the past 3 years.<br /><br />Result: Myrnin is back to being a cruel lunatic and won't let anybody near his machine (he still thinks it's Ada in there), Amelie and Oliver don't get along, Michael refuses to believe he's a vampire (and nearly gets killed when he walks out into the sunlight), Shane thinks his sister it still alive, Eve thinks she still lives at home, and... nobody remembers who Claire is, except for Oliver. He and Claire seem to be the only ones left with their memories intact. And 3 of The Core Four don't know they are double dating and living together.<br /><br />I enjoyed this book, but in my opinion, those 4 people got back together <i>way</i> too soon. It seemed forced and way too easy. (soul mates, anyone?) Michael and Eve look into each other's eyes and a chapter later they are back to making the neighbors blush. Same thing goes for Shane and Claire, Claire just needs to bat her eyelashes a few times and next thing you know they are a couple again, more or less.<br /><br />Claire keeps her memories, until very last second, but then Shane's father sacrifices himself and blows up the machine and: All is well again in Morganville. Except for Myrnin, who feels like hell and gets replaced by Claire. Who makes up for it by putting Shane's father's brain <i>in a jar</i>. Frank asks her not to tell Shane. <br /><br />*scans the horizon* Poor Claire, it won't be pretty when this thing blows up in her face...</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3033849479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12898329734349954269">Claire and Mernan fix the machine that controls the boundaries and other special controls of Morganville, but something goes wrong and both humans and vampires are affected - they seem to be losing their memories and in some cases, their minds. Claire is one of the only ones not affected and she must battle nearly the whole town to reach the machine to turn it off.<br/><br/>This was another fun installment in the series. The author definitely created an interesting new threat for Morganville, though the s</span>
  <span id="freeText12898329734349954269" style="display:none">Claire and Mernan fix the machine that controls the boundaries and other special controls of Morganville, but something goes wrong and both humans and vampires are affected - they seem to be losing their memories and in some cases, their minds. Claire is one of the only ones not affected and she must battle nearly the whole town to reach the machine to turn it off.<br /><br />This was another fun installment in the series. The author definitely created an interesting new threat for Morganville, though the story did drag in a few places as the teens ran around town trying to figure out the problem - though I guess that is to be expected to be realistic. If they just fixed the problem immediately, it would make for a very short book. <br /><br />I think what I found most interesting with regard to the characters this time around, was how we got a glimpse of what is going on between Amelie and Oliver. We've known for a while now that they have some kind of history and they are often at odds. We learn a little more about them and it is like a teaser for future drama. I am hoping future books give us more of that story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12898329734349954269" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText18198878230709956360" style="display:none">I really liked the plot for this one! Now that Ada isn't around to run the machine that controls Morganville, Mernan is linked to it and of course things go haywire because he isn't the most stable person. Humans and vampires start to lose time, they think they're three years in the past. Michael forgets he's a vampire, Mernan is feral, Amalie hates Oliver. Claire is one of the only people not affected and she has to find a way to shut the machine down. <br />The plot moved quickly and the story was fun. I enjoyed seeing the younger versions of Michael, Shane, and Eve and how they reacted to Claire. The ending had a twist and I'm looking forward to the next book. </span>

  <span id="freeText6507092833704741253" style="display:none">I simply adore this series! Above everything I adore the friendship between Claire, Shane, Michael and Eve. How they watch out for each other and the light and fun way they interact. Always teasing each other but still you feel the love. <br><br>We are back in Morganville and in the beginning all seems easy going, which would be a new thing for Morganville. But then Claire and Shane run to rescue Eve from a Party and suddenly Claire finds herself looked in Myrnins Lab to finish the work on the "machine" . The machine that takes the memory from people that leave and tries to keep them leaving in the first place. <br><br>Myrnin is the craziest character ever and I love him, in a weird way ;) <br><br>But then Claire realizes that something is off with the people and she thinks the machine is causing it. People loose their memory and forget about the last 3 years. This is not only sad but dangerous! Claire has to act fast, but again Vampire politics come in the way. Then her friends loose their memory too and Clair is alone. This was the heartbreaking part of the story, when all begin to loose their memory and Claire is all alone. <br><br>I'm totally in love with those books and the next one can't come soon enough. If you haven't pick them up yet, why waiting? <div id="review_1385373325" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1385373325" />
    <a title="Lorna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10620039-lorna"><img alt="Lorna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1341183135p2/10620039.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1385373325?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lorna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lorna" href="/user/show/10620039-lorna">Lorna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10620039-lorna?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10620039-lorna?shelf=paranormal-favorites">paranormal-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10620039-lorna?shelf=best-ya">best-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10620039-lorna?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1385373325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17899105588160986163">4.5/5 stars I continued with this series by listening instead of reading. As usual with any of the books in this series, I got pulled into the story and didn’t want to stop listening. It had just been long enough since I read the first eight books almost back to back, to completely engage me all over again. Morganville, the town that these books take place in, is a town run by vampires. A town where human’s can’t leave, and where the taxes they pay are at the blood bank. Great premise!<br/><br/>Claire is </span>
  <span id="freeText17899105588160986163" style="display:none">4.5/5 stars I continued with this series by listening instead of reading. As usual with any of the books in this series, I got pulled into the story and didn’t want to stop listening. It had just been long enough since I read the first eight books almost back to back, to completely engage me all over again. Morganville, the town that these books take place in, is a town run by vampires. A town where human’s can’t leave, and where the taxes they pay are at the blood bank. Great premise!<br /><br />Claire is still working with Myrnin, otherwise known as an on again/off again crazy, very old vampire-also considered by many as the best character of these books.They have been working on getting the machine that takes care of the town back up and running. No matter that he thinks that using Claires brain would be just the thing to make the machine work. Of course, that would mean that Claire would no longer have a body. Since they had to do away with Ada, the last person that had her brain attached to the machine, Myrnin, has been grieving for her. Of course, as always, Claire is involved in all the inner workings of the town. Not because she’s a vampire-she isn’t-but because not only is she a teenage genius, but she has become a sort of favorite of the town founder, Amelie-but not always in a good way. When the problem with the machine is solved, you would think things would be smooth sailing for our feisty heroine. That couldn’t be further than the truth. It never is in Morganville.<br /><br />Once again, this author has come up with another intricate plot to keep Claire, her boyfriend Shane, and her friends Eve and Michael, right smack in the middle of another mystery and more than enough action, and yes, even more deaths of both the human and vampire kind. College students attend the Rave from Hell, and of course Claire, Shane, and Eve are right in the middle of it. Not to mention that everybody seems to be having lapses of memory. Something weird, or rather weirder than usual, is happening in Morganville.<br /><br />Narrator Cynthia Holloway was very good, as far as the female voices, but her male voices weren’t the best, in my opinion. She just didn’t make her voice go deep enough. However, it wasn’t that big of a problem, and I would listen to one of these by her again. Like I said, I was completely drawn into the story, and that has to be partly due to the narrator.<br /><br />These books are not only for young adults, but for anyone that enjoys good writing, plotting, wonderful characters,a sweet(sometimes lustful romance), and snark, all surrounded by the horror of living in a town controlled by vampires. Ms. Caine is an excellent storyteller, and these books should be a must read for anyone that enjoys a paranormal story.<br />Highly recommended!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17899105588160986163" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1143535951" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1143535951" />
    <a title="Brandi Kosiner " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2614253-brandi-kosiner"><img alt="Brandi Kosiner " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593741913p2/2614253.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1143535951?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi Kosiner " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi Kosiner " href="/user/show/2614253-brandi-kosiner">Brandi Kosiner </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1143535951" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18119065182091214615"> I wanted to read this one because it has been my personal pleasure in the last of 2014 (read this one end of December). I love the vampires, the relationship between our main character Claire, who is wicked smart and able to roll with the punches, and her hot boyfriend Shane. It has been heating up a lot and I love each book where they become closer through shared experiences. The mad scientist Myrnin is always fun and surprising to read about. The leader of the town Amelie and 2nd in command O</span>
  <span id="freeText18119065182091214615" style="display:none"> I wanted to read this one because it has been my personal pleasure in the last of 2014 (read this one end of December). I love the vampires, the relationship between our main character Claire, who is wicked smart and able to roll with the punches, and her hot boyfriend Shane. It has been heating up a lot and I love each book where they become closer through shared experiences. The mad scientist Myrnin is always fun and surprising to read about. The leader of the town Amelie and 2nd in command Oliver always are mysterious and their motives and goals seemingly ever changing. I love the plots and has been so fun to read. <br /><br /> The plot and pacing in Ghost Town did not disappoint. I read half of it in one night and would have read more if my meds didn't knock me out like a blow to the head. Claire finds herself in horrible situations again with impossible choices. It really tipped the power, and made her doubt if the new gained freedoms were all for show. And then the unthinkable happened and I was like oh my gosh. We learned so much from this one encounter and I felt such at a loss because some of the things that I thought wouldn't change in the series did. <br /><br /> Claire shows her raw intelligence and will power to survive and protect her friends once again in this one. And I keep on admiring her ingenuity, and loyalty. We get to see to the heart of some of the characters when their memories are stripped three years. We see their actions as they struggle to deal with the losses that they are feeling all anew, the people they are now surrounded by where the relationship dynamics have changed if they even remember them at all. <br /><br /> Most of all though, the theme of redemption ran through this one. There are some sacrifices I never saw coming as well as alliances formed that aren't really expected. The action and character development was non-stop and it kept me entertained and engaged. <br /><br /> The ending was shocking and even though I probably should have seen parts of it coming, I didn't and when I reached the last page, I immediately wanted the next book in my hands.<br /><br />Bottom Line: Beloved characters facing all new challenges and range of emotions</span>
  <a data-text-id="18119065182091214615" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/329251883" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/329251883?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mello ❣ Illium ✮Harry✮ ☀Myrnin☀ Torin Ichimaru" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mello ❣ Illium ✮Harry✮ ☀Myrnin☀ Torin Ichimaru" href="/user/show/6981505-mello-illium-harry-myrnin-torin-ichimaru">Mello ❣ Illium ✮Harry✮ ☀Myrnin☀ Torin Ichimaru</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/9605136-ghost-town">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6981505-mello-illium-harry-myrnin-torin-ichimaru?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6981505-mello-illium-harry-myrnin-torin-ichimaru?shelf=vamps">vamps</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6981505-mello-illium-harry-myrnin-torin-ichimaru?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6981505-mello-illium-harry-myrnin-torin-ichimaru?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6981505-mello-illium-harry-myrnin-torin-ichimaru?shelf=hawt-heroes">hawt-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6981505-mello-illium-harry-myrnin-torin-ichimaru?shelf=sassy-heroines">sassy-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6981505-mello-illium-harry-myrnin-torin-ichimaru?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6981505-mello-illium-harry-myrnin-torin-ichimaru?shelf=mello-s-may-challenge">mello-s-may-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer329251883" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3249995634497694303">I stayed up way too late reading this. I couldn't stop. I just had to know what caused this new problem, although I'd known it was Myrnin, somehow and I just had to know how Claire was going to fix it.<br/><br/>Honestly, though, why does Rachel Caine insist on torturing Shane? That guy cannot win.<br/><br/>Morganville was once again in chaos. Everyone was losing three years worth of memories and while this happened, everyone closest to Claire turned on her because they just couldn't remember who the hell she was. I</span>
  <span id="freeText3249995634497694303" style="display:none">I stayed up way too late reading this. I couldn't stop. I just had to know what caused this new problem, although I'd known it was Myrnin, somehow and I just had to know how Claire was going to fix it.<br /><br />Honestly, though, why does Rachel Caine insist on torturing Shane? That guy cannot win.<br /><br />Morganville was once again in chaos. Everyone was losing three years worth of memories and while this happened, everyone closest to Claire turned on her because they just couldn't remember who the hell she was. I honestly could not figure out wth Claire was going to do to fix this. She thought it was her fault, but turns out, it wasn't at all. I'd even thought that maybe in her fatigue (because of Amelie's punishment) that perhaps she'd messed something up. Turns out, it was Myrnin's grief over Ada that brought this about. Just like Claire, I knew it was a horrible idea on Amelie's part that Myrnin be the vamp he's mind was interfaced with that machine. Boy were we both right.<br /><br />In the end, Claire's allies came from two of the least likely people. Luckily, even though Shane lost three years and was pretty awful to Claire at first, he came around. You could tell that he just knew something was still there. Poor Michael, though. Forgetting you're a vampire and walking out into the sun. That was just awful.<br /><br />To fix things, the most unexpected person made a huge sacrifice to set things back to as normal as Morganville could get. Too bad Myrnin and that same person's brain ended up burdening Claire with a sick secret. I love Myrnin, but I can see why Claire resents and even hates him at times. I know why he told her about it. He'd wanted to do things this way the entire time. If he and Claire had just listened to each other, maybe that bit of madness wouldn't have happened. Still, if Shane ever finds out, I expect Armageddon.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3249995634497694303" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_128086661" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/128086661" />
    <a title="Kelly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/251943-kelly"><img alt="Kelly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1385315310p2/251943.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/128086661?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly" href="/user/show/251943-kelly">Kelly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/251943-kelly?shelf=physical-books">physical-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/251943-kelly?shelf=signed">signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/251943-kelly?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/251943-kelly?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/251943-kelly?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/251943-kelly?shelf=read-in-2010">read-in-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/251943-kelly?shelf=2010-favorites">2010-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer128086661" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14413748702178865270">One of the things that I've consistently enjoyed about this series is that I don't ever feel like I'm overwhelmed by how heavy the reading is. Is it because the writing is extremely accessible? Is it because the plot is very fast-paced? Maybe it's both. I just know that I sit down to read these and I come out of it with a smile.<br/><br/>Part of it comes from the characters. Claire is strong, smart and brave. She is willing to put herself on the line consistently for those around her. Not just her friends</span>
  <span id="freeText14413748702178865270" style="display:none">One of the things that I've consistently enjoyed about this series is that I don't ever feel like I'm overwhelmed by how heavy the reading is. Is it because the writing is extremely accessible? Is it because the plot is very fast-paced? Maybe it's both. I just know that I sit down to read these and I come out of it with a smile.<br /><br />Part of it comes from the characters. Claire is strong, smart and brave. She is willing to put herself on the line consistently for those around her. Not just her friends. Everyone in town. For Myrnin. For Amelie. Even for Oliver, who she mostly loathes.<br /><br />I really enjoyed the arc in this book. It took the events of the last two books and made them mean something. And we were given resolution to several little threads that had been hanging around. That's always nice. The characters, especially Claire, continue to grow. Even the vampires are branching out and trying to change.<br /><br />I loved the book, I love the series. I'm eager for MV #10.<br /><br />-Kelly @ <a href="http://paranormalbookreviews-kelly.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Reading the Paranormal</a></span>

<div id="review_93450853" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/93450853" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2783046-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487873283p2/2783046.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/93450853?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/2783046-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer93450853" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12426342238353100714"><br/><br/>I must start out by saying that I devoured this book in mere hours. Rachel has pumped up the creepy factor in Morganville to 1000 in Ghost Town! If you thought the vampires in Morganville were devious, evil, kill-all-humans before, just wait until you see them now! This book has twice the random attacks, twice the RUN FOR YOUR LIFE moments, and best of all TWICE THE MYRNIN!!!!<br/>For those of you out there with an undying love of Claire's super crazy boss, Myrnin, you will be excited to know that My</span>
  <span id="freeText12426342238353100714" style="display:none"><br /><br />I must start out by saying that I devoured this book in mere hours. Rachel has pumped up the creepy factor in Morganville to 1000 in Ghost Town! If you thought the vampires in Morganville were devious, evil, kill-all-humans before, just wait until you see them now! This book has twice the random attacks, twice the RUN FOR YOUR LIFE moments, and best of all TWICE THE MYRNIN!!!!<br />For those of you out there with an undying love of Claire's super crazy boss, Myrnin, you will be excited to know that Myrnin is once again front and center for Ghost Town! But sorry guys, that's all the spoilery info I'm giving out today! Just trust me when I say that October 26th you need to RUN, not walk, to your nearest bookstore and get the newest addition to the Morganville Vampires! Rachel has,once again,out-done herself! Ghost Town was exciting, creepy, riveting, and,most of all, filled with Myrnin!!! My only complaint about the book, not enough Bob. lol</span>
  <a data-text-id="12426342238353100714" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('um9pvfrWRtspPM8U0ZGh+wd5+nIwVWbLQ07/6cfkMd6ASQBvQYiPs44Xe3UmZKsk0SYduv7Y6KwYMLlYCqfDRA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vnUqwPiA3TcdvCUaI828w5zIK1VkXkQQsNbt1+FTsE2EU0MSQ94UX7qXkXvUOLYcSpfMnarTynfrqKtmLBBC1w==')})
  }
//]]>

But when one of Mab\'s spells mistakenly taps into a powerful, long-dormant curse, she finds her magic spinning out of control - and crashing right into Will Sanger, a boy from town. \n\nWill has always relied on the logical, tangible things in his life, like his dogs, his soccer team, and even his complicated family. So he tries to dismiss all he sees and feels around Mab. Still, the strangeness and beauty of her magic draw him in. \n\nAs Will and Mab grow closer, the unbound curse grows stronger. Hiding in the shadows of the forest, it seeks to manipulate Will and gain Mab\'s power - even if that means destroying everything they love.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"12550619525761320273\"
